Foreigners Spying on Fortresses in Shimonoseki, Japan

A Consul of a Certain Country Is Suspected

Japan Temporarily Adopts a Cautious Attitude

According to Japanese news, the Kanmon area of Japan is very convenient for spies to infiltrate, so many spies from various countries are secretly active. The Shimonoseki Land and Sea Police Station and the Gendarmerie are on high alert. Recently, a deputy consul of a certain country and his wife were found to be suspected of spying on the fortress area. The police authorities are very concerned. The deputy consul came to Shimonoseki from Tokyo and stayed in a hotel. He secretly obtained a map of the General Staff Headquarters from Shimonoseki to a certain place in Sanin. He walked from Shimonoseki to a certain place in Sanin to investigate the terrain. His wife also used the excuse of training her pet dog to sneak into Mt. Hi and other important areas of the fortress every day to spy on the terrain and communicate secretly with her country. Because he is a consul of a major country, the Japanese authorities do not want to handle it rashly, which may cause a major international problem, and are temporarily adopting a cautious attitude. (World Press)

US Navy Layoffs Rumor

Is This a Prelude to a Major Reform?

(Washington) The reduction of officers in the US Navy Fleet and Marine Corps is now in full swing again. Today, the report of the Special Inspection Group recommends that the peacetime reduction of the Navy Fleet and Marine Corps be based on the terms of the report. Marine Corps officers will be reduced from 1,093 to 991. Officers who have reached the age of retirement are all on the list of those to be removed. However, the report also advocates that the number of Navy Fleet officers should not fall below 5,499. According to the Navy's mobilization plan, in order to achieve the effect of land contact, the current 5,499 Navy Fleet officers are still 1,318 short of the number needed to operate the country's warships. The report continued that the number of drivers on each warship must be 80% full, and this policy must continue to be maintained. The report strongly opposed other reforms of the Navy. Although the so-called other reforms were not explicitly stated, they actually implicitly referred to the merger of the US Coast Guard Fleet and the US Navy Fleet. If the merger is realized, the personnel of the Coast Guard Fleet will receive the same treatment as the Marine Corps. Since the news of the layoffs came out, the Marine Corps officers have been deeply surprised, because Marine Corps Commander Fro recently made a proposal to expand the Marine Corps based on the weakness of the Marine Corps. Fro also pointed out that the officers of the Marine Corps have served for 13 years, which is more than twice the experience of the officers of the same rank in the Navy Fleet. (15th National Telegraph)

Because this conference was initiated by the government, the British delegation therefore submitted a report to the government yesterday afternoon. Soviet Administrative Reform

Eliminating Bureaucratic Habits

Strengthening Individual Responsibility

(Moscow) The Soviet government has promulgated an order on the organizational plan of administrative and economic structure. The order aims to ensure the specific leadership of the administrative and economic work of various departments of the Soviet Union, its application to the new tasks of the reconstruction period, and the elimination of bureaucratic habits. The order sets out various specific measures for administrative personnel to strengthen the system of single management and individual responsibility for their assigned tasks. For example, in addition to the elected Soviet organs, the number of trusts in various administrative and economic tasks should be reduced, and the council system should be abolished. Each People's Committee will be presided over by one People's Commissar, and the number of its Deputy Commissars shall not exceed two. Each People's Committee shall be composed of 40 to 70 members, at least half of whom are representatives of local organs and enterprises, and it is stipulated that regular meetings shall be held once every two months. (16th TASS Telegraph)

U.S. Government Conducts In-depth Study, Silver Policy Unchanged

(Washington) After a lengthy discussion with Representative Sumners today, Treasury Secretary Morgenthau issued a statement saying that after a detailed study of the silver issue, the Treasury Department deeply feels that the issue of increasing the value of silver is worthy of research. He said that the Treasury Department is constantly conducting in-depth research on the silver issue and ultimately feels that the London Silver Agreement is actually not easy to implement in terms of stabilizing the value of silver. He has always advocated openness on the silver issue. If the economic situation gradually improves, we should affirm this principle and proceed accordingly. He has always believed that the silver issue is the only way to alleviate the economic panic. Now that everything is gradually on the right track, it is even more inappropriate to change course. According to recent reports, the U.S. price index has been increasing rapidly, faster than any other country, so he firmly advocates that the government should not suddenly change its policy, and if President Roosevelt deems it necessary, he can definitely effectively implement the silver issue. He also said that recently, some people engaged in silver mining are taking advantage of the rising silver prices to engage in speculation, which is deeply concerning.

(National Telegram, 15th)

Situation in Spain Remains Unsettled

Shocking New Discoveries in French Mega-Fraud Case

Antarctic Expedition Encountered Danger

Plane Damaged, Crashed, Western Team Member Seriously Injured

Little America (Antarctica) The famous American Antarctic Expedition, led by Rear Admiral Richard Byrd, encountered a major disaster today. Four members of the expedition were flying when the plane's engine suddenly broke down. Captain Saros Beck urgently turned the plane back to its original base and sent a wireless report to the mother ship. However, the plane crashed into the tundra covered with ice before reaching the mother ship. The fuselage was destroyed, and all four members of the expedition were seriously injured. Fortunately, the crash site was not far from Byrd's temporary camp. (National Telegram, 16th)

American Fugitive Missing, Greek Interior Minister Resigns

Athens The inside story of the disappearance of the American Insull has been revealed. The authorities learned today that Insull took the Greek postal ship Nicholas to Piraeus on Wednesday. His wife said today that Insull had recently been in contact with a London lawyer, and that on Wednesday a British man visited him to arrange his departure from Greece. (Reuters, 16th)

Death of Dr. Black, Head of the Department of Anatomy at Peking Union Medical College

(Beiping) Dr. Black, head of the Department of Anatomy at Peking Union Medical College, passed away last night at the age of forty-nine. Dr. Black was a Canadian who came to Beiping in 1919. He believed that primitive humans could be found in Asia. He accidentally discovered a human tooth at Zhoukoudian, forty miles from Beiping. Dr. Black determined that the tooth belonged to a kind of primitive human, and then began excavating. He eventually discovered the bones of ancient humans, which are now known as "Peking Man." Dr. Black did very important scientific work on this. British, American, and Chinese science magazines often published his works. Dr. Black had been ill for several months and was always worried about dying before the research on "Peking Man" was completed, so he urgently wanted to continue his research. The doctor recently allowed him to work two hours a day, but Dr. Black often did not follow his advice. He entered his office at five o'clock last night and worked at his desk as usual. When the doctor entered this morning, he had been dead for a long time. Those who heard the news lamented his death. (Special Telegram, 16th)

The New Life Movement in the Capital

—Promoting Association Established Yesterday—

Wang Zhaoming and Thirty-One Others Elected as Supervisors

(Nanjing) The inaugural meeting of the Capital New Life Movement Promotion Association was held at 9:00 am on the 16th at the Lizi Society. More than 500 people attended, including initiators Wang Zhaoming, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Lifu, Ye Chucang, Wang Shijie, Fang Juehui, Chu Minyi, Luo Jialun, and guests from all walks of life. Zhu Jiahua presided over the meeting, led the salutation, and delivered a speech, roughly stating that since Chairman Chiang initiated the New Life Movement in Jiangxi, various places have responded one after another, which proves that the New Life Movement meets the requirements of the times. He also said that the New Life Movement is suitable for Chinese history and is based on the consistent spirit of the inherent morality, propriety, righteousness, integrity, wisdom, benevolence, and courage. Everyone should start from themselves, strive to practice, and can revitalize the nation. Then Fang Juehui reported on the preparation and solicitation of initiators. Subsequently, Ye Chucang encouraged comrades to not be afraid of difficulties, to vigorously promote the New Life Movement, to find happiness in suffering, and to realize the New Life with sincerity and perseverance. Wang Zhaoming gave a speech, saying that Chiang originally advocated starting the New Life Movement in Nanjing first, but various places responded spontaneously, which shows that everyone needs to demand this movement. However, in order to prevent it from becoming propaganda of slogans and slogans, or fearing negligence in practice, the first thing to do in implementing the New Life Movement is to be honest and the second is to be scientific, using scientific methods to control life. Finally, Luo Jialun, Chu Minyi, and Wang Shijie gave speeches successively, and Wang Zhaoming and thirty-one others were elected as supervisors. (Central News Agency, 16th)

Kong and Sun Return to Capital Together

The Fulton was towed into Haichuan Bay yesterday and has lost its original shape. At 9:00 PM tonight, forty-eight hours after the initial fire, smoke still lingers. The ship is still a dangerous object, as there is still a powder magazine on board that was not watered down when the accident occurred. (16th Reuters Dispatch)

Inner Mongolia Autonomous Committee Temporarily Located at Bailing Temple

Mongolian Representative Talks After Returning to Beiping

Autonomous Region Also Defined

Beiping Correspondence: The thirteen representatives of the Inner Mongolian leagues and banners who came to Beijing, including Nima Ote Sor, Guote Zhuoerzhabu, Gongchuke Lashi, Zhao Taibao, Sengge Linqin, Jierge Lang, Ayuerzhana Ayuer, Cangsen, Linqin, Bai Yincang, Gu Zhaozong, and Su Ludai, returned to Beiping by car on the morning of the 14th at 11:00 AM. This morning (14th), they separately visited Huang Fu and He Yingqin and urged He to concurrently serve as the Chief of Guidance for Inner Mongolian Autonomy. According to Nima, "Inner Mongolian autonomy has experienced many twists and turns. Through the mediation of President Wang and Chairman Jiang, eight principles were finally established, and the autonomy measures were announced, resulting in an exceptionally satisfactory outcome. The representatives are scheduled to stay in Beiping for three days. After visiting Chairman Huang and Chairman He, they will return to Bailing Temple to begin organizing the Inner Mongolian Autonomous Political Affairs Committee in accordance with the organizational outline. All members are determined not to concurrently serve as department or division chiefs. The autonomous region is currently limited to the seven tribes of the Western Four Leagues and the Three Special Banners. In the future, we still hope to include the Eastern Three Leagues. We heard in Beijing about the request from the left and right wings of Qinghai to join the Autonomous Political Affairs Committee, but the details are not very clear. After the Chahar department is reorganized into a league, the system of each league and banner will continue to follow the hereditary method without any changes." Zhao Taibao also said, "The Organic Law of the Inner Mongolian Local Autonomous Government stipulates that the Autonomous Government is located in Bailing Temple, but this is temporary. In the future, a suitable location will be selected based on national defense, economy, population, and other conditions. The representatives have drafted a budget for the expenses of the Political Affairs Committee, temporarily set at 50,000 yuan per month, which only covers administrative expenses, and does not include military expenses or construction expenses. This budget has been reported to the Executive Yuan but has not yet been approved, although there will likely be no major changes in the future. The central government intends to grant De Wang an important military position in Inner Mongolia and is currently discussing it." Guote Zhuoerzhabu also said, "My trip to Jiangxi was purely to request instructions regarding the issue of the Japanese forcibly establishing radio stations in Mongolia. Wang and Jiang both expressed that they would convene a meeting to discuss it, presided over by the central government, and would never allow the Japanese to enter Inner Mongolia by even an inch." The so-called Eastern Three Leagues in Nima's speech refer to the Jerim, Zhaowuda, and Zuosotu Leagues within Liaoning and Rehe, while the Western Four Leagues refer to the Xilingol, Ikhe Zhao, Ulanqab, and Chahar Leagues. The Three Special Banners are the Tumote, Ejina, and Alxa. (14th)

(March 14th)

Hai Shun Steamer Traveling Between Fujian and Hong Kong Runs Aground

More Than Two Hundred Passengers Rescued

Stern Flooded, Now Aground on Reef

Xiamen Correspondence: The Hai Ning, Hai Cheng, Hai Yang, and Hai Shun steamers of the Hong Kong British firm Jardine Matheson & Co. ply between Hong Kong, Shantou, Xiamen, and Fuzhou. On the 11th, the Hai Shun steamer left Xiamen from Fuzhou. At 8:00 PM, it ran aground on a reef in the Baiyouyang sea area. All 216 passengers were rescued. According to those who escaped and arrived in Xiamen, the process of the accident was roughly as follows: the Hai Shun steamer completed loading its cargo at about 1:00 PM on the afternoon of the 11th, and the departure procedures were also completed. It could have departed immediately, but the captain hosted a banquet, which lasted until after 3:00 PM. Then, the wheels were turned and the steamer departed. At about 8:00 PM, it passed through the Baiyouyang sea area, which has the Changkeng Gorge, shaped like a tripod, with many hidden reefs in the middle. The navigator mistakenly took the wrong route, causing the steamer to run aground violently on the reef. At that time, the tide was high and the reef was low. Fortunately, the bow did not break through, but with a loud crash, passengers lying on the bunks or canvas beds in the cabins all rolled onto the deck. For a moment, cries, shouts for help, and the sound of the waves echoed each other, and order was lost. The captain hurriedly put the ship in reverse, but with too much force, the stern struck the reef again, piercing a hole. Seawater gurgled in, and the steamer was grounded and could not get out, and the stern was sinking. The captain began to send wireless telegraphs and launch flares for help. The Xiamen Customs patrol boat and the naval vessel that was nearby received the report and arrived first. The fishing boats also heard the flare and arrived. The passengers boarded the lifeboats, then the patrol boat, or the fishing boats. It was around midnight, with dark clouds and heavy rain. Approximately 160 people boarded the patrol boat, and the rest boarded the fishing boats. Fortunately, all 216 passengers were rescued. At 6:00 PM on the evening of the 12th, they sailed to Mawei. Those who rode the fishing boats landed in Mawei, and the patrol boat sailed directly to Fuzhou. The captain, crew, and a dozen sailors remained on the steamer. After the Hai Shun incident, Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Hong Kong headquarters received a distress telegram and immediately telegraphed the Xiamen branch, instructing them to send a steamer to assist. After receiving the telegram, the Xiamen branch sent the Hai Ning, which was docked in Xiamen, to assist. The merchant steamer Jiahe, which was passing by after leaving the Hai Shun, also moored next to the Hai Shun to guard against pirates. The Jiahe only sailed to Xiamen on the evening of the 12th, when the Hai Ning arrived. It is also heard that the stern of the Hai Shun is flooded to a depth of more than 30 feet, and the engine room and power station are completely submerged. Half an hour after running aground, all the electric lights went out. Currently, only the cargo in the bow is preserved, and the stern is flooded. It is expected that it will not be easy to get the steamer out of danger after unloading. The steamer has a deadweight of approximately 2,000 tons. (March 14th)

Tao Liu Love Suicide Case Supreme Court Rejects Appeal

Beijing News: The sensational Tao Sijin, Xu Qinwen, Liu Mengying love suicide case, which occurred over a year ago, has concluded. After the Zhejiang High Court's retrial judgment, the prosecutor appealed, and it is now learned that the Supreme Court has ruled to reject the appeal. The original text is recorded below:

Facts: Tao Sijin and Liu Mengying were both female students at the Zhejiang Art College. Initially, they shared the same dormitory, and their friendship deepened through late-night conversations. Subsequently, a romantic relationship developed. At the height of their passion, they vowed never to marry men in order to maintain their love for each other. As time passed, mutual suspicion arose. Liu Mengying noticed that Tao Sijin was unusually close to Liu Wenru, a female teacher in the drawing department of the school, and suspected that they also had a lesbian relationship. She repeatedly urged Sijin to break off relations with Liu Wenru, and threatened to kill Liu Wenru or Tao Sijin, or to reveal their love history. As a result, their relationship gradually deteriorated. Xu Qinwen was a close friend of Tao Sijin's deceased brother, Tao Yuanqing. After Yuanqing's death, Xu Qinwen, admired by Chinese and foreign figures for his paintings, raised funds to purchase land and build a house in the Lotus Pavilion area of West Lake to display his works. He also built several houses next to it for his own residence. Liu Mengying often visited Xu's residence with Tao Sijin. During winter and summer vacations, the two women would stay at Xu's place together, a fact known to his family. In the winter of the tenth year of the Republic of China, the art college was on holiday. Tao Sijin returned to her native Shaoxing, and Liu Mengying went to Shanghai to visit her sister, Liu Qingxing. Due to the outbreak of the war in Zhabei, Shanghai, Liu Mengying fled to Hangzhou on the night of February 3rd of the 21st year of the Republic of China and went directly to Xu Qinwen's residence to stay. On the 6th of the same month, Tao Sijin, upon receiving a letter from Liu Wenru informing her of her intention to return to Sichuan, also brought food from Shaoxing to Hangzhou to see her off. After meeting Liu Mengying at Xu Qinwen's residence, she stayed at the art college for two nights. On the afternoon of the 8th, she planned to return to Shaoxing, passing by Xu Qinwen's residence. Due to Liu Mengying's persuasion, she did not leave. The two women stayed together for three nights without any unusual behavior. On the 11th, Tao Sijin again wanted to return home, but was persuaded by Liu Mengying to stay. In the afternoon, Xu Qinwen took his girlfriend, Guo Dehui, to the Jianggan Beixian Bridge school to cover for his sister. Only Liu Mengying, Tao Sijin, and the maid Chen Zhugu were at home. Liu Mengying asked Chen Zhugu to heat water for her bath. Because she needed snow cream, she and Tao Sijin asked Chen Zhugu to go out and buy it. Tao Sijin gave Chen Zhugu six jiao (dimes). After Chen Zhugu left, Tao Sijin bolted the front door and read the newspaper in the bedroom. After her bath, Liu Mengying again questioned Tao Sijin, asking if she had come to Hangzhou to see Liu Wenru. She also said that if she did not change her ways, a tragedy would surely occur. Tao Sijin told her not to be so stubborn. She then went to the outer room of the bathroom to fetch an electric stove to boil tea. Liu Mengying followed her, nagging incessantly. Tao Sijin, in a moment of anger, was overcome by homicidal intent. She ran to the kitchen next door, grabbed a kitchen knife, and slashed at Liu Mengying. Liu Mengying also grabbed a wooden stick to defend herself. They fought around the showroom, blood splattering everywhere. Liu Mengying, wounded, dropped the stick and ran to the front door, trying to open it and escape, but was caught up by Tao Sijin, who knocked her to the ground and cut her trachea, causing her immediate death. Tao also fainted on the ground. Chen Zhugu and another friend, Qiu Benyuan, returned and called at the door without response. Shortly after, Xu Qinwen and his sister, Xu Xianye, also arrived, but were still unable to enter. They walked along the river to the back door, forced it open, and entered, finding Liu Mengying murdered on the ground, and Tao Sijin also lying there. They immediately opened the door, called the police, and reported to the local police station, which reported to the prosecutor of the Hangzhou County District Court, who examined the corpse and injuries, and initiated an investigation and prosecution.

Reasons: After reviewing the files, it is clear that the victim, Liu Mengying, died from being murdered, as verified by the prosecutor in the first instance, who filled out a post-mortem examination report attached to the file. The defendant, Tao Sijin, does not deny killing Liu Mengying. Their relationship began as a lesbian love affair, which then became fraught with mutual suspicion, and ultimately resulted in a conflict due to Liu Mengying's insistence that she break off relations with Liu Wenru, leading to the stabbing death. The cause of the conflict and the circumstances of the crime have been confessed by the defendant without reservation. Furthermore, there are the diaries of the two individuals and letters from Liu Mengying to Tao Sijin that can be consulted as evidence, making the facts extremely clear. The grounds for the appeal, concerning Tao Sijin's murder, state that after reviewing the statements of Xu Qinwen, Tao Sijin, and Chen Zhugu (i.e., Chen Zhugu), the lesbian relationship between Tao Sijin and Liu Mengying had long been fractured, leading to mutual attacks and infighting. The cause of the fracture was that Liu Mengying viewed Liu Wenru as a rival, and Tao Sijin also suspected Liu Mengying of having an affair with Xu Qinwen. When Xu Qinwen refused Tao's request to come to Hangzhou but allowed Liu Mengying to stay at his home, it was seen by Tao Sijin, who left in resentment. The motive for the murder was latent in this. Tao Sijin returned to Xu's residence on February 8th, repeatedly inviting Liu Mengying to go to Shaoxing, but Liu refused, and Tao also did not leave. On the afternoon of the 11th, Tao saw Xu Qinwen take Ms. Guo to Huaxian Bridge, believing that there was an opportunity to take advantage of. She then ordered Chen Zhugu to go to Qixia to buy snow cream, closing and bolting the door to prevent outsiders from entering. All of this is enough to determine that Tao Sijin's killing of Liu Mengying was premeditated. As for Tao Sijin's claim that Liu Mengying, after taking a bath, went outside and asked if she had come to Hangzhou to see Liu Wenru, this was the tone of the initial questioning. How could she not even put on her coat and shoes, and follow her to the tea room, nagging incessantly, and standing motionless, allowing her to grab a knife and kill her? It is also sufficient to show that when Liu Mengying was bathing, Tao Sijin was already holding a knife, waiting outside the bathroom, and as soon as she came out, she attacked her with the knife. The premeditation is very clear. This court believes that the facts of the crime should be determined based on evidence, and it is not appropriate to base the judgment on speculation. Although the relationship between Tao Sijin and Liu Mengying gradually deteriorated after mutual suspicion arose, judging from Tao Sijin's repeated statements, Xu Qinwen and Liu Mengying did not have any relationship. Therefore, Liu Mengying's stay at Xu Qinwen's home was not noticed by Tao Sijin. Furthermore, Xu Qinwen did not know that Liu Mengying had come to Hangzhou in advance. His letter preventing Tao Sijin from coming was before Liu Mengying's arrival, so there was no issue of welcoming or rejecting her. The grounds for the appeal, stating that Tao Sijin's motive for murder was latent in this, are clearly inconsistent with the facts. As for Liu Mengying's suspicion that Tao Sijin had a lesbian relationship with the female teacher Liu Wenru, viewing her as a rival, as evidenced by Tao Sijin's diary of October 12th of the 20th year, and Liu Mengying's angry words on a postcard to Tao Sijin in Shanghai, her emotions were on the verge of collapse, which can be proven. However, after examining the statements of Chen Zhugu, Qiu Benyuan, and Xu Qinwen in the first and second trials, they all stated that when Tao Sijin first arrived at the house, she sat and talked for a short time, then took a basket to stay at the art college. She returned to their home on February 8th, originally intending to return home, but did not do so due to Liu Mengying's persuasion. On the 11th of the same month, she again wanted to return home, but stopped because Liu Mengying persuaded her to stay. Therefore, Tao Sijin's delayed departure was due to Liu Mengying's earnest retention, so how could it be said that her failure to leave was because she had the intention to murder when the opportunity arose? Moreover, according to what Chen Zhugu and Qiu Benyuan said, Tao Sijin stayed at Xu Qinwen's house for three nights, talking and laughing as usual, without any quarrels. Sometimes they went to the market together, and returned together, without seeing anything else unusual. This observation is also very different from the behavior of someone who is plotting murder. As for Liu Mengying asking the maid Zhugu to buy snow cream before taking a bath because it had run out, according to Chen Zhugu, Tao and Liu were together at the time, so it cannot be presumed that Tao Sijin intentionally made her leave. As Chen Zhugu's trip to the Qixia market was because there were no good products to buy near Zhaoqing Temple, it was not Tao Sijin's intention to go there. Closing the door when going out was the usual habit of the Xu residence, as Xu Qinwen also stated clearly without any difference. It is also difficult to recognize that Tao Sijin was preventing others from entering in order to achieve her purpose of killing. As for the location of the murder, according to the first trial's map, the bloodstains began near the door inside the corridor. If, as the grounds for appeal stated, Tao Sijin was already holding a knife, waiting outside the bathroom, and could not do so because the door was closed, then as soon as Liu Mengying came out after taking a bath, she attacked her with the knife, the bloodstains should have started outside the bathroom door. How could she wait for her to walk near the corridor before raising the knife towards her? Therefore, Tao Sijin's statement that Liu Mengying returned to the bedroom after taking a bath, and asked her again if she had come to see Liu Wenru, arguing with each other, and that she went to the outside of the bathroom to fetch an electric stove to boil tea, and Liu followed her again, nagging incessantly, leading to a conflict, using a knife to kill her, is still credible. In summary, there is no evidence in the whole file that Tao Sijin premeditated the murder. The original trial recognized that her intention to kill arose temporarily, and punished her according to Article 282, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Also, because the crime occurred before March 5th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, according to Article 2 of the Amnesty Act, the sentence was reduced by one-third, sentencing her to life imprisonment, and proclaiming lifelong deprivation of public rights in accordance with Article 292 of the Criminal Law. The facts and the law are properly applied, without any impropriety. The grounds for appeal are purely based on speculation and are difficult to justify. As for Xu Qinwen's part in the seduction, according to the survey form of the art college, although the victim Liu Mengying was still under the age of 20, her stays at Xu Qinwen's home were not denied by the defendant. However, Article 257 of the Criminal Law states that the crime of seduction requires the person seduced to leave the custody of the person with parental rights, guardian, or curator, but the offender must have the intention and act of abduction, or transfer the person seduced under his own control, with a purpose of achieving a private gain, to be able to establish the crime. After reviewing the files, Liu Mengying often stayed at Xu Qinwen's house with Tao Sijin during school holidays, purely out of her own volition, and was not summoned by Xu Qinwen. On February 3rd of the 21st year of the Republic of China, when Liu Mengying fled from Shanghai to Hangzhou, she went directly to his residence, which was also unknown to Xu Qinwen in advance. Regardless of whether his family knew the location of her whereabouts, it is clear that Xu Qinwen had the intention and act of abduction, and it cannot be clearly pointed out that he had any private gain. Therefore, it does not meet the requirements for establishing the crime of seduction. The original trial proclaimed Xu Qinwen innocent, without any inappropriateness. The grounds for the appeal, stating that Xu Qinwen continuously seduced a woman under the age of 20 to leave the supervision and protection of the person exercising her parental rights, and criticizing the original judgment as improper, are also difficult to recognize as justified. Based on the above conclusions, the judgment should be made according to Article 408, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, as the main text.

Songjiang

Tragic Death of a Man Who Did Not Work

In Wuku Township, under the jurisdiction of the county, there was a man named Wu A'gen, whose elder brother, Xiulong, was in the fruit business. A'gen was adopted by his aunt's husband, Guo Fuxiu, at a young age. He was addicted to pleasure and did not work. In recent years, he had mortgaged and sold almost all of his own property. After being adopted, he changed his name to Guo Dimei. Recently, after his family property was exhausted, he pawned his house to Xie Shutang. Guo went to Xie's house on the 26th day of the tenth lunar month of last year to borrow 500 wen (cash), a custom known as "adding charcoal." However, Xie's wife, Peng, refused. Guo Dimei played a prank, lying down in Xie's kitchen. Peng waited until he was asleep, secretly summoned four people, and, carrying iron towers and hoes, severely beat Guo's head, causing serious injuries to the back of his head. He died immediately. They then used a flour sack to hold stones and tied it to Guo's body, sinking it in the Yaojing Bridge (i.e., the 30th Foreign Bridge) River. It was not until the other day that his brother, Xiulong, was informed and went with a friend to investigate and report to the Tenth Tu Dibao, who reported to the Prosecutor's Office. Yesterday, Inspector Wang was dispatched to the countryside to examine the body. Guo's body was lifted, although not rotten, it was swollen like a water buffalo. After receiving the report, the court, based on Xie Peng's confession, immediately summoned Xie Peng for interrogation. The other perpetrators have fled without a trace.

Suzhou

The Fifth District Office of Hengjing Burned Down

The Fifth District Office of Hengjing Town, whose buildings were recently purchased, consisting of four courtyards, was unfortunately burned down on the evening of the 15th. A district clerk, Rong Sheng, was adding oil to a kerosene lamp when he was careless, causing a fire. The first three courtyards, with nine large rooms, were completely destroyed. All files were placed in the fourth courtyard, which was fortunately preserved. Another district clerk, Zhang Deshun, bravely rescued the telephone when the fire was raging, causing burns to his arm. The district chief, Kong Xian'gao, has reported the disaster to the county government for record.

Scattered Bandits Discovered on the Suzhou-Wuxi Canal

The Suzhou-Wuxi Canal is an important waterway in Jiangnan. Ferries travel back and forth like weaving. Recently, scattered bandits have been discovered in Wangting and other places along the canal, making travel very dangerous. The Suzhou-Wuxi Water and Land Public Security Bureau, in order to maintain water security, has dispatched a police team from the land public security forces to patrol along the road. On the water public security side, six patrol boats from the water public security district have set out to cruise in order to prevent any accidents.

Wuxi

The Director of the Provincial Office Comes to Wuxi to Supervise the Account Inspection

Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department of Jiangsu Province, believes that there are many abuses in the collection of land taxes in various counties. Recently, a case of embezzlement of more than 40,000 yuan occurred in Liyang County. If personnel are not sent to investigate and verify the accounts, it will not be enough to eliminate this abuse. Yesterday, this county delegated Wu Gengyu to come to Wuxi to supervise the account inspection, going directly to the county government to meet County Magistrate Yan and inquire about the current situation of land taxes. County Magistrate Yan immediately accompanied the land tax director, Zhu Kaiguan, and the second section chief, Fei Yunnong, to the Yigui cash collection counter and the account book office to inspect in detail. In addition to the already pardoned incomplete accounts, from the 4th to the 15th year of the Republic of China, which have been calculated by the staff of the account book office by year and night, the remaining current accounts from the 16th to the 22nd year are audited by Director Wu and his assistants, who personally audit them in the account book room to see if there is any embezzlement. Once the accounts are inspected, they will be listed and reported to the Provincial Finance Department for review. During the account inspection period, villagers who go to pay land price tax will be issued a small ticket.

After the former director of the Second Public Security Bureau, Wang Xiezhong, was dismissed for losing firearms, the county magistrate transferred Fan, the former director of the Fourth Bureau, to fill the position. After Fan took office, he reorganized the police affairs, and public opinion was pleased. Having been in office for five months, he has been repeatedly accused, and after investigation by the County Public Security Bureau, he was dismissed. The vacant position was transferred to Gao Chongshan, the original director of the First Bureau. Liu, unwilling to obey the order, took the seal and all important documents to the province to appeal, leaving only his wife, Li, to stay in the bureau. When the new Director Gao and Zhang Yu, the Inspector of the Public Security Bureau, arrived at the bureau to take office, Liu's wife, Li Rongzhen, refused to hand over, and even slammed the table and scolded. Gao was helpless and went to the county government to ask County Magistrate Yan for instructions. County Magistrate Yan believed that Liu had already gone to the town, and the affairs of the Second Bureau were extremely important, so he ordered Director Gao to start working first. If Liu's wife made any more trouble, she would be sent to the county court for strict legal action. It is said that Liu's wife, Li Rongzhen, is a sister to the concubine of Gu, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, so she is fearless and shows great female power.

Jia Yu, the director of the Wuxi Tooth Tax Collection Office, resigned after being approved by the Provincial Education Funding Management Office because the tax revenue was not prosperous and the handling of affairs was difficult. He Shuzhai and Sun Shihe were sent to the county jail for custody. On one hand, the county telegraphed the provincial management office, urging them to send personnel to Rugao to guarantee that Jia Yu would come to Wuxi to clean up the account, in order to value the tax money.

Jiading

The Biological Mother Poisoned Two Daughters

Gao Jieren, of the Xijia Fence in Nantai Street, once served as the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce. In the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, he married a Guangdong merchant's maid, Chen, in Shanghai as his third concubine. At first, they were very harmonious, and had two daughters. The eldest daughter, He, was seven years old, and the youngest daughter, Ming, was five years old. Recently, Chen lost Gao's favor for some reason, so their relationship deteriorated and they often quarreled. On the 15th, Chen suddenly said that she would commit suicide to trouble Gao. Gao feared that an accident would happen, and had the door of her bedroom removed. Chen became even more angry, saying that Gao maliciously wanted to freeze her to death. Gao then had the door reinstalled. However, Chen had already prepared opium ashes and green vitriol. At about 10 o'clock, she first tricked her two biological daughters into swallowing it, and then she also ate it herself. The maid, Wang Ma, saw the situation from outside the door and rushed to tell Gao. Gao quickly hired doctors Xu Pingdu and Geng Shiting to examine them. They were diagnosed as having been poisoned and were immediately treated separately. The youngest daughter died of poisoning at about one o'clock. The eldest daughter died at seven o'clock on the morning of the 16th. Chen has been rescued and is now calm and there is no danger to her life, but she still refuses to eat. At the beginning of the incident, Gao reported to the County Public Security Bureau, which reported to the County Government. Xue Bingyang, Director of the Public Security Bureau, Chen Youmin, Secretary of the County Government, and Shao Ling, the trial judge, went to investigate that night. The Gao family is now preparing coffins and is formally requesting an autopsy.

Joint Automobile Transport on the Nanjing-Wuhu Line

The long-distance automobile transport routes in Jiangsu Province are divided into three sections: Nanjing-Wuhu, Shengju, and Suzhou-Jiading. The Nanjing-Wuhu line is currently underway. It is divided into east and west sections. The east section is directly under the Highway Administration Office, and the west section is contracted by the Wuhu Long-Distance Automobile Company. The contract is signed by both parties and the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau. A draft agreement has been prepared and will be submitted to the office for approval. Twenty long distance transport vehicles have been purchased, and they will be delivered around the end of the fourth month. The implementation period is about the end of April. If the Nanjing-Wuhu line is successful, the Shengju and Suzhou-Jiading lines will continue to be implemented.

Sun Tonggang Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

The purpose of the Aviation Society is to promote aviation education so that all men, women, and children in the country have the opportunity to try flying, and young aspirants have a place to learn. In recent years, although the domestic aviation industry has been vigorously promoted, civil aviation, due to business considerations, cannot provide the general public with widespread opportunities to try flying. Military aviation, also due to military considerations, cannot take this into account. American Merchants Need Tungsten Ore

Entrusted the International Trade Bureau to Introduce

The export situation of tungsten ore has gradually declined in recent years. American Aserf Metal Products Company, etc., need a large amount of tungsten powder and crushed tungsten. Due to the recent reduction in transportation, they specially wrote to the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry to introduce them. After receiving the letter, the bureau immediately notified tungsten merchants to list prices according to type for contact. Tungsten ore is produced in Chongyi, Dageng, Nankang, Shangyou in Jiangxi, and Zixing, Rucheng, Yizhang, Binxian in Hunan, etc. Due to banditry in Jiangxi Province in recent years, the output has decreased, only reaching about 6,000 tons per year. As for the export quantity, in 1932, 5,525 piculs were shipped from Shanghai to Germany, 2,357 piculs to the United Kingdom, 24,200 piculs to Hong Kong, 1,677 piculs to Italy, 420 piculs to France, and 155 piculs to Singapore and other places. But since 1932, the export quantity has been far less than before and is too small to be investigated for a while.

Italian Loan Guarantee Securities Postponed

Ministry of Finance Continues to Pay Off Loans as Usual

After sixteen major banks in this city undertook the 44 million large loan from the Ministry of Finance guaranteed by the Italian Boxer Indemnity, they negotiated with Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi to issue company-type securities with a value of 30 million yuan, guaranteed by the Italian Boxer Indemnity pledged by the Ministry of Finance. In addition, a syndicate jointly formed by the Ministry of Finance and the banks and the sixteen major banks will provide joint and several guarantees. A special office has been set up on the third floor of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and Zeng Rongfu, the advisor to the Ministry of Finance, has been hired as the Secretary-General. All progress procedures have been planned and finalized. The issuance, originally scheduled for April 1st, has been decided to be changed to April 15th. According to reliable sources, this type of security is a novelty in our country, so the progress procedures must be extremely cautious. The issuance regulations have not yet been approved by the Legislative Yuan, so the issuance has to be postponed. As for the 44 million yuan that the Ministry of Finance borrowed from the banks, which was originally scheduled to be paid off in four months, the banks are still paying off on schedule.

Financial Circles Discuss the Shanghai Commercial Crisis

Money Shops Reduce Dealings

All Industries Face More Difficult Turnover

Since the January 28th Incident, the vitality of Shanghai's commercial sector has been depleted and difficult to recover in a short period of time. For more than two years, most shops have been operating miserably and barely maintaining the overall situation. However, with the surge of new banks established last year, in order to expand their business, lending has been slightly relaxed, which has allowed various businesses to rely on turnover and barely manage to support the remaining market. Unexpectedly, this year, at the beginning of the lunar year, the financial sector, affected by last year's business, has seen many who have declared liquidation. Even those who are still operating normally, seeing the sluggish market and lack of vitality, are bound to be mutually vigilant and strictly review lending. According to insiders in the industry, the practices of

money shops of opening current accounts with various shops, regardless of new or old, will be strictly rectified this year. Therefore, around the Lantern Festival this time, the number of current account openings has dropped sharply by two-thirds (for example, each shop had 600 accounts last year, but this year only 200 have been opened, and for shops with thousands, only 300 have been opened). Therefore, shops with slightly inferior reputations find it more difficult to turn over. Since there are no other ways to use funds, those who have no choice but to declare liquidation are numerous. However, there are also several large shops that are related to the overall situation that want to liquidate but cannot support themselves, resulting in rent arrears of more than ten months. The courts, in order to protect the overall situation of the city, are unwilling to comply with the creditors' requests to issue seals, and there are even more of these. If this continues, according to our observations in the financial sector, the silk cocoon season next month will be ignored, and the overall situation in Shanghai will be in imminent danger.

Page 12

Our Country's Trade with France

Can Still Maintain a Trade Surplus

Our country's trade with France has always been advantageous. This is because France exports mainly luxury goods, but in recent years, due to economic collapse and weak purchasing power, sales have been quite narrow. Our country's exports, on the other hand, are mainly agricultural products and minerals, so we can still maintain a trade surplus, which is the most glorious event in our country's foreign trade. However, because merchants do not know how to improve, trade is becoming increasingly bleak. A reporter from the Dagong News Agency learned about the trade situation between our country and France from relevant parties yesterday, which is recorded below.

Our Country's Trade Situation with France

Trade between France and China has never been very developed. The reason is that the rural economy has been bankrupt for many years and purchasing power is weak. Therefore, French goods exported to China, such as cosmetics and other luxury goods, are only patronized by women in cities, resulting in the value of imported goods declining day by day. Our country's goods exported to France, on the other hand, are mainly agricultural products and minerals, which are necessary items for French industry. Other items have decreased compared to before because merchants do not know how to improve. There are many basic raw materials for industry in the country, and France has repeatedly investigated our country's authorities. Our country is indeed vast and rich in resources, but unfortunately no one pays attention to it, so it has not been able to be sold abroad.

Comparison of Trade in the Last Two Years

The total value of French goods transported to China in 1932 was 99,262,000 francs. The total value in 1933 was 134,159,000 francs. The total value of our country's exports was 209,891,000 francs. The total value in 1933 was 244,820,000 francs. Comparing the total value of imports and exports in the past two years, our country's trade surplus in 1932 was 110,629,000 francs. The trade surplus in 1933 was 114,661,000 francs.

Major Import and Export Items

French exports to China are mostly metal products, accounting for 35% of the total value. The next is steel plate, estimated at 15%. The next is paint, accounting for 7%. Chemicals and wool each account for 3%. Our country's exports to France are mostly agricultural seeds, accounting for 40% of the total value. Peanuts are next, accounting for 13%. Other rattan ware accounts for 4%. Chinese tea accounts for only 1.5%.

France Levies Import Tax on Chinese Tea

Our country's foreign trade has always been dominated by silk and tea. The value of Chinese tea exported to France is quite large. In recent years, due to a lack of improvement in planting and poor packaging, the color, aroma, and taste have been slightly worse than before. Also, due to the dumping of foreign tea, the export of Chinese tea to France has fallen sharply recently. Last year, the value of Chinese tea transported to France was only more than 3 million francs. Recently, reports have stated that the French government plans to levy an import tax on Chinese tea. However, according to the French Commercial Counselor in Shanghai, he has not yet received the relevant

order from his country. The International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry also denies this news.

Banking Sector Explains That the Total Amount of Silver Does Not Include Silver Coins

150 Million Taels Refers Specifically to Silver Bars and Sycee

Silver Coins Have Many Varieties and There Are No Statistics on Circulation

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that since Japanese bankers in the city previously announced that the total amount of silver in the country was 150 million taels, it has caused a misunderstanding among the general public. In fact, since it is referred to as a certain number of taels, it only refers to the sycee and large bars used to mint silver coins. Silver coins that have already been minted and silver jewelry are not included. As for the number of silver coins, there are many varieties, both new and old, making it difficult to accurately count them, so they are not listed. If it is said that foreign banks hold two-thirds of the silver, it is because silver dollars and pure silver have different purities. Storing silver bars or sycee is more cost-effective than storing silver dollars, and it does not mean that foreign banks intend to manipulate the banks. The facts are stated as follows:

Fearing Misunderstandings, a senior figure in the banking sector made a statement to the visiting reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency yesterday, saying that the total amount of 150 million taels of silver is indeed accurate. However, after reading it, the general public without knowledge can easily misunderstand or mistakenly believe that the number includes silver coins, which may cause adverse effects on society. Therefore, it is specifically stated that the number does not include silver dollars, and even jewelry is not included. It refers specifically to the sycee or silver bars stored. Therefore, the words "taels" in the number are the most obvious, because silver dollars, etc., should not be referred to as taels. As for the silver stored by foreign banks, which accounts for two-thirds of the total, it is because silver dollars and pure silver silver bars and sycee have different purities. Storing silver bars or sycee is more cost-effective than storing silver dollars, and it does not mean that foreign banks store more silver in order to manipulate the silver market. Even if they want to manipulate it, it is impossible to be fully prepared. The banknotes issued by Chinese banks all have sufficient reserves, and must be investigated by the government and deemed suitable. The detailed number is reported in detail by each bank every week, and can be publicly investigated by anyone. The amount stored this week is about 319,990,000 yuan. As for the statistics of silver coins in the country, there is no way to find out. There are many types of silver coins. Those currently circulating on the market include Qing coins, common dragon dollars, Yuan coins, Sun Yat-sen founding commemorative coins, base coins (commonly known as foreign coins), Spanish coins (commonly known as standing figure foreign coins), and the new Sun Yat-sen image silver coins minted by the mint. There are many types, and they are scattered and difficult to trace in various places. Therefore, it is impossible to statistically calculate the details. The rumors of a total of 300 million are also unreliable.

New York International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation Announces Last Year's Profit

According to a letter from the Shanghai Telephone Company, the New York International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation reported to its shareholders on the 15th of this month the following profit situation at the end of last year: Income for 1933 was $73,959,947.51 (compared to $67,526,838.61 in 1932); expenditure was $61,529,147.17 (compared to $60,096,510.62 in 1932).

Net income was $12,430,800.34 (compared to $7,430,327.99 in 1932); expenses of various associated companies, general interest, and interest on bonds of the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation totaled $11,736,674.75 (compared to $11,365,288.21 in 1932). Net profit for 1933 was $2,894,125.59, compared to a net loss of $3,934,960.22 in 1932, representing a business turnaround of $4,629,085.81. As of December 31, 1933, there were 6,399,002 shares of the company's stock held by the public. Based on the 1933 net profit, each share could receive a dividend of 11%.

Memorial to the Loyal Souls and Unknown Heroes Who Died in the Shanghai Battle to Be Constructed

Funding Portion Already Fully Raised

The Design of the Mausoleum Is Extremely Tragic and Grand

Construction to Commence after Approval and Be Completed in Six Months

During the January 28th Incident two years ago, our troops fought bitterly for more than thirty days. The villages around Miaohang in the Shanghai-Songhu area were completely destroyed under the intense fire of cannons and machine guns, and the soldiers died in heaps. This battle record is truly the most glorious manifestation of the national spirit. Considering that most of the soldiers and volunteer civilians who were crushed to pieces at that time died without their names being known, leaving only desolate mounds, various sectors of this city, could not bear to see these many unknown heroes fade into obscurity. Therefore, they decided to build a Tomb of Unknown Heroes and launched a fundraising campaign to comfort the loyal souls and to perpetuate their memory for eternity.

Design Completed, Solemn and Grand

The tomb was designed by the architectural advisor of the municipal government, Dong Dayou. According to Mr. Dong's statement to the Shen Shi News reporter yesterday, all aspects of the tomb site design have been completed. The tomb site is located in Miaohang Town, where the Shanghai battle's artillery fire was most intense and sacrifices were greatest, covering an area of approximately thirty acres. The entire tomb area is shaped like a sword, including a tomb hall and a large stone retaining wall, with stone steps in between, appearing extremely solemn and grand. The surroundings of the tomb will be planted with flowers and trees, and roads will be built around it, connecting to Dachang in the west and Lingnan Road in Zhabei in the south, so that those who come to pay their respects will not have the inconvenience of detours.

Erecting a Stone Stele to Perpetuate History

Since the remains of the generals and soldiers of the Shanghai battle have already been transported to the capital and buried at the foot of Zijin Mountain, this tomb is purely commemorative in nature. Inside the hall, only a stone stele, more than ten feet high, will be erected, inscribed with the Shanghai battle and the process of establishing the tomb, for future generations to pay their respects. On the walls around, various souvenirs of the war at that time, the clothing and portraits of the martyrs, and various things related to the fallen soldiers that are worth keeping as historical memorials will all be collected and displayed within, so that the extremely tragic and cruel foreign insults suffered during the Shanghai battle can forever leave a deep impression in the minds of future generations.

Raising Funds and Commencing Construction on Schedule

Regarding the funding part, it has recently been raised. In addition to the thirty acres of land donated by various sectors of Baoshan and the ten thousand silver dollars donated by the Shanghai Municipal Citizens' Local Maintenance Association, the remainder was raised by donations from various sectors. It is learned that the fundraising campaign has reportedly been concluded by various banks, raising approximately tens of thousands of dollars. The shortfall has been supplemented by a telegraphic transfer of 20,000 dollars in subsidies from the Executive Yuan of the National Government. The estimated construction cost of the tomb is more than 50,000 dollars, so most of the funding has already been secured. Architect Dong will submit the design drawings to the preparatory committee for review in the next few days, and construction will begin immediately. It is expected that it will be completed in six months, at which time an extremely tragic and grand completion ceremony will be held.

The original text is excerpted below: To Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, and Chairman Jiang of the Military Affairs Commission, with respect: Our Fujian has suffered years of corrupt government and bandit disasters, the local area is devastated, and the people are suffering unspeakably. Shareholder of Xingtai Foreign Firm Sues Manager

Result: Apology Settles the Matter

Zhou Jinyu, a native of Fenghua, Zhejiang, and manager of the Xingtai Foreign Firm at 3 Hankou Road, was recently sued in the First Special District Court by Deng Rengui, a shareholder of the firm, through lawyer Lin Yingqing, on charges of breach of trust. A trial has been held once. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi presided over a continued interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Division. According to the plaintiff Deng Rengui, the basis of his lawsuit was that the defendant jointly opened the Xingtai Foreign Firm in November of the 19th year of the Republic [1930], with him serving as manager and the plaintiff serving as deputy manager. Unexpectedly, the defendant, harboring malicious intentions, established another company, Xinfeng, to do Xingtai's business, and on November 16 of last year, he privately sent a letter to a British London client, stating that Xingtai would definitely go bankrupt at the end of the lunar year, deliberately destroying Xingtai's reputation and disregarding the law. He should be punished for breach of trust. When questioned, Zhou Jinyu admitted that he had been a shareholder with two thousand shares when Xingtai was founded and had served as manager, but he had not established another company, Xinfeng. The content of the letter he wrote to the client did not match what the plaintiff said. Now, after mediation by friends, he is willing to publish an apology in the newspaper, etc. Judge Wu ordered a rescheduling and instructed the defendant to publish an apology in the newspaper within five days.

Second Participation in the Chicago Fair to Commence in Mid-Next Month

Council Decides to Revise the Labeling of Products

Based on the Principle of Attracting International Market Attention

Last year, the products from our country participating in the Chicago Exposition won considerable praise from people in the United States. This year, the association still intends to hold it, and our country has also decided to participate again. The Liaison Association stationed in Chicago, after the executive director returned to the country, has each been working separately, soliciting products. Recently, Council Member Zhou Guanrong went to Jiangxi to collect products and has now arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Sound News Agency visited him and received the following account of the process:

Focus on Displaying Products　　Last year, most of the exhibits from our country participating in various displays tended to focus on culture and art. It was only when the conference opened that it was learned that the products sent by other countries to participate were mostly focused on international trade. Although we won good reputation at the time, we did not get any real benefit in terms of trade promotion. Therefore, after the council decided on the exhibits to participate in this session, it was decided to focus on our country's porcelain, cotton, paper, summer cloth, and other famous products from various places that can attract people's attention in the international market. A small number of exquisite products with cultural value will also be taken along.

Convening of the Council Meeting　　When the reporter further inquired about the date of departure, it was said that it must wait until the council meeting is convened before it can be determined. The approximate travel date is in mid-April. The reason why he came to Shanghai so urgently this time was that he received a Shanghai telegram in Jiangxi, so he rushed here. Unexpectedly, Council Member Dong Kunfan has not yet returned to Shanghai from Fujian because of collecting products and arranging other matters, so the meeting could not be held immediately. It is expected that Council Member Zhou will also come to Shanghai in the next few days. Finally, the reporter further inquired about whether it was true that the ancient instruments from the Beijing Observatory would be transported to Chicago for display. According to reports, this matter was requested by the Chicago Exposition on behalf of the Chicago Planetarium. This matter is currently being negotiated with the government. As long as they are carefully protected during transportation, it is expected that the government will not object.

According to the New Sound News Agency, Li Monong, the son-in-law of Central Committee Member He Xiangning, was arrested on suspicion of being a communist. Since being brought to the Public Security Bureau on the 13th, Central Committee Members Wu Zhihui, Liu Yazi, and others went to bail him out but were unsuccessful. The next day, according to Director Peng of the Special Affairs Section of the Public Security Bureau, Li Monong confessed that evening that he was a communist because of numerous witnesses and material evidence that could not be denied, but he refused to surrender. He was transferred to the Garrison Headquarters that night. However, when reporters inquired at the Longhua Songhu Garrison Headquarters, they said that he had not been sent there and was still detained in the Public Security Bureau. According to reliable information obtained by the New Sound News Agency reporter yesterday, Li Monong was sent to Nanjing on the 14th.

Wanxiang Crashes Into a Barge

All Boatmen Rescued

The Sanbei Company's Wanxiang ship sailed from Hankou to Shanghai yesterday. At 9:50 AM, it entered the Wusongkou, and at 11:30 AM, it arrived at the Huangpu River. Near the Customs Wharf, just as it was riding the high tide, the captain, Liu Xunda, proceeded according to the route. The ship turned around the Waitan River surface outside the Waitan Bridge and moved south. There was a large barge loaded with coal coming out of Lujiazui and heading to Pudong to unload. The Wanxiang was moving fast with the tide, and Captain Liu urgently pulled the horn and ordered it to give way, but the barge could not retreat, and the Wanxiang did not have time to reverse, resulting in a collision. The bow of the Wanxiang hit the center of the barge, causing it to overturn immediately. The cargo and boatmen in the barge all fell into the water, and the barge's hull was pinned down by the Wanxiang's bow and could not be shaken off for a while. All the boatmen, including the captain, who fell into the water were rescued by nearby small sampans and water patrol boats. Fortunately, they were all rescued, but the cargo was completely lost. As for the barge that collided with the Wanxiang's bow, a small Jianghai Customs tugboat came forward and managed to tow it down, then dragged it to the Huangpu River and parked the broken barge there. Afterwards, the rescued boat captain reported to the Jianghai Customs Port Affairs Office and the Water Patrol Team and negotiated with the Sanbei Company for compensation.

Hu Yazhou Mixes Into Court and Openly Instigates Testimony

Aftermath of the Case of Using Counterfeit Currency

Hu Detained in Court for Investigation According to Law

Han Shoushan, a Chinese detective from the General Police Station, previously arrested a man named Wei Zichun for using counterfeit currency. Forty-one counterfeit five-yuan banknotes were found next to the child Wei was carrying. He was sent to the First Special District Court, which, after investigation, sentenced him to five years in prison. Unexpectedly, Wei was not convinced and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yu and Assessors Jiang and Zhou opened a court hearing. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated the circumstances of the case, and also stated that the girl Wei was carrying at the time has now been summoned to court by the police, and she can prove everything herself. At this time, Hu Yazhou, sitting in the audience, suddenly approached the girl and whispered to her. Detective Han Shoushan noticed this and reported it to Judge Yu, saying that Hu's suspicious behavior seemed to be instigating testimony and should be noted. Judge Yu then summoned the child for questioning, but she stammered and hesitated. After strict questioning, the child still refused to tell the truth. The court then summoned Hu Yazhou and asked him about his address, occupation, and reasons for coming to court. Hu initially claimed to be a coal broker, then said that he was a runner for lawyer Shen Fuxiang. Since the Shen lawyer requested by the appellant was introduced by him, he came to court to listen. After reviewing the confession, Judge Yu felt that Hu was very ingratiating and had been seen in court more than once. He also recalled that this person had recently testified in court in another case. He then ordered the case files to be checked. It was then discovered that when Wu Zhongwu and Fang Yixian's case of embezzlement and appeal was opened, Hu was one of the witnesses in the case. However, when checking his testimony that day, it was discovered that there was suspicion of perjury. He felt that Hu usually mixed into the court under false pretenses, solicited lawsuits, instigated testimony, and made perjury his duty, which was not allowed by law and should be thoroughly investigated and severely punished to warn against cunning and treachery. Therefore, after the trial of Wei Zichun's case was concluded, Hu Yazhou was immediately handed over to the detectives and taken to the police station for investigation and prosecution according to law.

Large Fire in Zhabei Again Yesterday

Seventy to Eighty Thatched Sheds Destroyed on Guangzhao Road

Around 4 AM yesterday, a fire broke out again behind the house of Su Chengdong, a native of Yancheng, who lived in a thatched shed at the intersection of Guangzhao Road and Hengfeng Road in Zhabei. In an instant, the flames spread in all directions and could not be controlled. The residents of the sheds and the residents of the tile houses along Hengfeng Road were awakened from their sleep in alarm, crying and screaming, and the order was in chaos. Fortunately, the police officers at the four-district two-branch police station learned about it early and telephoned the fire brigade, which drove the fire engines to the scene to extinguish the fire. It was extinguished at more than 6 AM. All seventy to eighty thatched sheds there were almost completely burned down, and the surrounding tile houses were not affected, which was also fortunate. Later, the police officer on duty at the station took the fire starter, Su Chengdong, to the station. According to his confession, he was 53 years old and had five family members, including his children and his elderly wife. For some reason, the rapeseed stalks placed behind his house suddenly caught fire this morning. After being alerted by people shouting, he tried to press down hard with clothes, but it was ineffective, leading to this disaster, etc. After the interrogating officer reviewed the confession, since the case was related to a fire, he immediately prepared a document and sent it to the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau of Zhabei for disposition. Later, the reporter found out that the location of the fire was bordered by Guangzhao Road to the north, municipal houses along Hengfeng Road to the west, and tile houses also connected to the east and south, and most of the tile houses had fire insurance. Fortunately, it had just cleared up after several days of rain, and the fire engines arrived quickly, otherwise the consequences would have been unimaginable. The area of the fire was about ten acres, and the number of people affected was about one thousand.

Preparation Process of the Nanshi National Goods Department Store

More Than Thirty Participating Manufacturers Display in Departments

Uniform Pricing to Cultivate Merchant Ethics

Wang Xiaolai and Wang Tingsong Hosted the Press Last Night

The Nanshi National Goods Department Store of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to open on the 21st of this month. Yesterday at 6 PM, Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Yansong, and others, hosted reporters from various newspapers in the city. During the dinner, Wang Xiaolai and Wang Yansong reported on the preparation process, saying, "Distinguished guests, we are very happy that you are here today. The reason why we have invited you here to talk is about the Nanshi National Goods Department Store. We want to rely on you to promote it widely in the newspapers to promote national attention. Our association has an unshirkable responsibility to promote national goods and sell domestic products in business terms. In the 20th year of the Republic [1931], we set aside a part of the product exhibition hall to establish a department store, which achieved remarkable results. Now, in view of the urgent national crisis, the promotion of national goods must be strengthened. Therefore, we founded the Nanshi National Goods Department Store at the former site of the county chamber of commerce on Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi. It has been several months since the preparation, and it is now roughly ready and decided to be officially opened on the 21st of this month. Now, I will briefly report to you on the preparation process.

Duties　The reasons why our association organized the department store have been mentioned earlier. After deciding to establish the Nanshi National Goods Department Store, we immediately appointed Mr. Yang Zhenxin to be in charge, appointed various staff members, and set up a preparation office on the third floor of the exhibition hall.

Registration　After the staff and office were decided, registration began on January 16. At that time, those who heard the news and participated were quite enthusiastic, such as China Enamel Factory, Asia-Pacific Electrical Appliance Factory, Qiming Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Huafu Hat Factory, Huahua Silk Bureau, China Chemical Industry Society, Heji Biscuit and Canned Food Company, Du Jinsheng Silk Weaving Scenery Factory, Guangdong Brothers Rubber Factory, Shengsheng Pasture, China National Goods Company, and more than thirty other companies.

Decoration　When our association started registration, on the one hand, in view of the fact that the former county chamber of commerce in Nanshi had been borrowed by government agencies, and the internal situation was not suitable for stores, we hired workers to renovate and decorate everything. The staff designed and planned to ensure that the form was new and suitable for the current situation.

Departments　The interior of the department store is divided into silk department, cloth department, woolen department, knitwear department, sanitary clothing department, candy canned food department, electrical appliance department, cosmetics department, sanitary products department, accessories toothbrush department, woolen straw hat department, ball shoes department, leather goods department, porcelain department, hardware department, copper department, local products department, clock department, cotton department, wool department, umbrella handkerchief department, silk scenery department, enamel department, thermos department, tobacco and alcohol department, stationery department, toy department, suit supplies department, and more than thirty other departments. The participating manufacturers are all the largest factories in Shanghai, and their products are exquisite and inexpensive. In the future, they will definitely arouse the interest of the people of Nanshi in using domestic goods, create a great force for domestic goods, and give foreign goods a great blow. Therefore, the order is neat and orderly, which cannot but be mentioned to you.　Cheap Price　The various goods in the department store are for the sake of promoting national goods. After the first meeting, it was decided that the goods should be cheap and of good quality, and there should be no bargaining, so as to cultivate merchant ethics and customer convenience.

Gifts　Moreover, the department store will also distribute gifts to all sectors of society at the opening, which is a small intention to promote national goods and is also sympathized with by all of you present. The above is the real situation of the preparation process of the department store. I hope that you will promote it widely in the spirit of promoting national goods. It is not only the fortune of the department store, but also the honor of the national goods industry.

Current Status of New Silone Forest Project

New Silone Wing On Forest Co., Ltd., since establishing a branch in Shanghai the year before last and issuing forest property certificates, has been quite trusted by the Chinese people, so in two years, a total of thousands of acres have been sold, with a selling price of 30 pounds sterling per acre. The company provides planting services without additional charges. According to the officially published softwood prices in the United States and Canada for the past 20 years, it is estimated that logging and selling after 12 years can yield a value of 250 pounds sterling. It is said that the soil and climate of New Silone are the most suitable in the world for planting pine trees. Its 12-year height averages 60 feet, with a circular diameter of 5 feet, and the growth rate is about four times faster than elsewhere.

Chinese Typewriter Patent Approved

Five Major Factories Actively Manufacturing

The Chinese typewriter invented by Yu Binqi, which is convenient for all walks of life, has been reserved patent by the government since the Republic of China 19th year, and approved for manufacturing. Since then, he has personally led workers to strive hard. In the past, due to the initial stage of establishment, the project was not perfect, and gradually improved. Especially in the National Goods Year, he contacted Shanghai National Goods factories to manufacture separately and personally reformed. In the past year, more than one hundred units have been produced, and sold out in ten months. With increased production, experience gradually increased, and technology greatly improved. After the disclosure in the newspaper, government agencies, banks, companies, and shops suddenly increased purchases. The factory is rushing to produce day and night, but it is still not enough to meet the demand. In order to precisely manage, the Yu Cooperative Factory Management Office is specially established at 541 Zhaofeng Road in Shanghai, in order to be close to the factory for easy guidance. Recently, the left and right movers of the machine have been changed from square to round, which is strangely sensitive. The newly produced steel characters, when typed on wax paper, can be mimeographed more than a thousand copies, and the ink is also more obvious, which is a world of difference from the products of the previous year. County Government Repairs Rural Roads and Bridges

The Shanghai County Government has now found that the rural roads in the county were originally very wide, but ignorant farmers, disregarding public interests, have either encroached on them for fields or occupied them as building foundations. Over time, they have become narrow paths, which really hinder people's travel. In order to rectify traffic throughout the county, it has already instructed the district chiefs to supervise and urge the township and village leaders to quickly investigate the original road requisition and use local manpower to build them wider. Bridges within their borders that have been in disrepair for many years and are damaged or collapsed should also be supervised and urged to repair them at any time. If there are any technical matters, they may request the county government to send personnel to guide them. The locations, dimensions, engineering, and reorganization plans for the roads and bridges that should be widened and repaired should be clearly reported for investigation.

Shanghai-Xuzhou Joint Transport Less-Than-Carload Freight Cars

To Be Implemented on April 1st

The Railway Bureau previously agreed with the Jinpu Railway that all Shanghai-Xuzhou joint transport less-than-carload freight cars would be directly escorted by personnel sent by both parties to ensure integrity. However, the two railway transport departments previously lacked sufficient escort personnel, resulting in the joint transport less-than-carload freight still being handed over in Pukou. The original plan has not yet been implemented. Now that the less-than-carload freight cars on this railway have been changed to be attached to regional passenger trains, the original freight dispatchers can free up three people to serve as Shanghai-Xuzhou joint transport less-than-carload freight escorts. However, it is still necessary to allocate eight workers to take turns serving on the trains. In order to facilitate the work, eight luggage porters from the Shangbei Station have been selected and trained. At the same time, an agreement has been reached with the Pulu Railway that the joint transport plan will be implemented on April 1st.

Wusong Whitebait on the Market

Recently, the weather has been sunny and warm, and the fishing season at Songkou has arrived. Therefore, the general fishing boats are all netting in the waters around the Three Gorges. In the past two days, some fishing boats have caught whitebait and brought them into port. Whitebait (commonly known as noodle fish) is white and fresh, and is a specialty of Songkou. However, in the early stages of the season, the supply is small, and it can only be sold in the fish shops in Songdi. It is rare to see it in Shanghai. The price of the fish is surprisingly high. Initially, it only cost one yuan per pound of fish. Yesterday, it has been changed to about two pounds per yuan. It is said that it will not be available for sale in Shanghai until a large number of fishing boats arrive in port.
